SELECT * FROM  (      select avg(AGE) as AGE,count(*) as NO_OF_DIAG , sum(PMNT_AMT) as PMNT_AMT, Y.DIAG_CD , max(DIAG_DESC) as DIAG_DESC from (select  A.POL_MBR_ID,EXTRACT (YEAR FROM B.BUS_DT) - EXTRACT (YEAR  FROM A.BRTH_DT)  as AGE , A.FRST_NM, A.MID_NM, A.LAST_NM , A.BRTH_DT, A.GEND_CD, B.CLM_ID, B.CLM_FORM_TYPE_CD, B.BUS_DT, B.CHRG_AMT,  B.ALLW_AMT, B.PMNT_AMT, C.DIAG_ID, D.DIAG_CD, D.DIAG_DESC from QART_EDW_BASE.POL_MBR A  inner join QART_EDW_BASE.CLM B on A.POL_MBR_ID = B.POL_MBR_ID and A.END_DT = date'9999-12-31'  inner join QART_EDW_BASE.CLM_DIAG C on B.CLM_ID = C.CLM_ID inner join QART_EDW_BASE.DIAG D on C.DIAG_ID = D.DIAG_ID and  D.END_DT = date'9999-12-31' ) Y group by  Y.DIAG_CD            ) Z order by NO_OF_DIAG  desc

MBR_ATTRBTN  where RUN_TYPE_CD = 'ROLLING' AND MBR_SRC_SYS_CD = 'IPP' AND ATTRBTN_TYPE_TXT <> 'UNATTRIBUTED'  AND rec_status_id = 1 and BEST_ATTRBTN_RUN_PRD_ROW_IND = 'Y' and PRSN_ID='3908234'

MBR_ATTRBTN WHERE OUTCM_BASE_REIMB_NBR ='OBR0004'    AND RUN_TYPE_CD='ROLLING' AND MBR_SRC_SYS_CD='IPP' AND ATTRBTN_TYPE_TXT <> 'UNATTRIBUTED' AND BEST_ATTRBTN_RUN_PRD_ROW_IND ='Y' AND REC_STATUS_ID='1' AND CLM_END_DT >= ( SEL ADD_MONTHS( MAX(CLM_END_DT),-2  )  FROM QA1_EDW_BASE.MBR_ATTRBTN WHERE  RUN_TYPE_CD='ROLLING' )   AND PRSN_ID='752293' QUALIFY ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY PRSN_ID ORDER BY CLM_END_DT DESC )=1

select diag_cd, B.diag_desc, count(*) from  QART_EDW_BASE.CLM_DIAG A inner join QART_EDW_BASE.DIAG B on A.DIAG_ID=B.DIAG_ID where B.END_DT = date'9999-12-31' group by B.diag_cd, B.diag_desc having count(*) > 1000 order by  count(*) asc

select  A.POL_MBR_ID,EXTRACT (YEAR FROM B.BUS_DT) - EXTRACT (YEAR  FROM A.BRTH_DT)  as AGE , A.FRST_NM, A.MID_NM, A.LAST_NM , A.BRTH_DT, A.GEND_CD, B.CLM_ID, B.CLM_FORM_TYPE_CD, B.BUS_DT, B.CHRG_AMT,  B.ALLW_AMT, B.PMNT_AMT, C.DIAG_ID, D.DIAG_CD, D.DIAG_DESC from QART_EDW_BASE.POL_MBR A  left outer join QART_EDW_BASE.CLM B on A.POL_MBR_ID = B.POL_MBR_ID and A.END_DT = date'9999-12-31'   left outer join QART_EDW_BASE.CLM_DIAG C on B.CLM_ID = C.CLM_ID left outer join QART_EDW_BASE.DIAG D on C.DIAG_ID = D.DIAG_ID and  D.END_DT = date'9999-12-31'  qualify rank() over( partition by D.DIAG_CD order by  A.POL_MBR_ID ) >100

select Y.DIAG_CD (   select  A.POL_MBR_ID,EXTRACT (YEAR FROM B.BUS_DT) - EXTRACT (YEAR  FROM A.BRTH_DT)  as AGE , A.FRST_NM, A.MID_NM, A.LAST_NM , A.BRTH_DT, A.GEND_CD, B.CLM_ID, B.CLM_FORM_TYPE_CD, B.BUS_DT, B.CHRG_AMT,  B.ALLW_AMT, B.PMNT_AMT, C.DIAG_ID, D.DIAG_CD, D.DIAG_DESC from QART_EDW_BASE.POL_MBR A  left outer join QART_EDW_BASE.CLM B on A.POL_MBR_ID = B.POL_MBR_ID and A.END_DT = date'9999-12-31'   left outer join QART_EDW_BASE.CLM_DIAG C on B.CLM_ID = C.CLM_ID left outer join QART_EDW_BASE.DIAG D on C.DIAG_ID = D.DIAG_ID and  D.END_DT = date'9999-12-31' ) Y  qualify rank() over( partition by Y.DIAG_CD order by  Y.POL_MBR_ID ) >100  having  Y.DIAG_CD ='787.91'

SELECT MBR_ID,GRP_ID,BILL_EXCL_EFFECT_DT                                 FROM uat3_ids_base.MBR_BILL_EXCL                                 WHERE SYS_OF_REC_ID=46                                 AND UPPER(PRDCT_CAT_CD) = 'M'                                 AND CAST ('2017-11-28' AS DATE FORMAT 'YYYY-MM-DD') = begin(LOAD_EFFECT_PRD)                  GROUP BY 1,2,3

SELECT BILL.MBR_ID,BILL.GRP_ID,BILL.BILL_EXCL_EFFECT_DT,PMBR.POL_MBR_ID                  FROM                                  (SELECT MBR_ID,GRP_ID,BILL_EXCL_EFFECT_DT                                 FROM uat3_ids_base.MBR_BILL_EXCL                                 WHERE SYS_OF_REC_ID=46                                 AND UPPER(PRDCT_CAT_CD) = 'M'                                 AND CAST ('2017-11-27' AS DATE FORMAT 'YYYY-MM-DD') = begin(LOAD_EFFECT_PRD)                  GROUP BY 1,2,3) BILL                 LEFT JOIN                                  (SELECT SRC_SYS_MBR_ID,SRC_SYS_GRP_ID,POL_MBR_ID                                  FROM uat3_edw_base.POL_MBR                                 WHERE SYS_OF_REC_ID=46                                 AND DATE'2017-11-27' BETWEEN STRT_DT AND END_DT                 GROUP BY 1,2,3) PMBR                  ON BILL.MBR_ID=PMBR.SRC_SYS_MBR_ID                 AND BILL.GRP_ID=PMBR.SRC_SYS_GRP_ID         GROUP BY 1,2,3,4
SELECT BILL.MBR_ID,BILL.GRP_ID,BILL.BILL_EXCL_EFFECT_DT,PMBR.POL_MBR_ID                  FROM                                  (SELECT MBR_ID,GRP_ID,BILL_EXCL_EFFECT_DT                                 FROM uat3_ids_base.MBR_BILL_EXCL                                 WHERE SYS_OF_REC_ID=46                                 AND UPPER(PRDCT_CAT_CD) = 'M'                                 AND CAST ('2017-11-28' AS DATE FORMAT 'YYYY-MM-DD') = begin(LOAD_EFFECT_PRD)                  GROUP BY 1,2,3) BILL                 LEFT JOIN                                  (SELECT SRC_SYS_MBR_ID,SRC_SYS_GRP_ID,POL_MBR_ID                                  FROM uat3_edw_base.POL_MBR                                 WHERE SYS_OF_REC_ID=46                                 AND DATE'2017-11-28' BETWEEN STRT_DT AND END_DT                 GROUP BY 1,2,3) PMBR                  ON BILL.MBR_ID=PMBR.SRC_SYS_MBR_ID                 AND BILL.GRP_ID=PMBR.SRC_SYS_GRP_ID         GROUP BY 1,2,3,4
